## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (homogeneous batch reactor ODEs)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time-derivative of a concentration A, which is the standard setup for kinetic rate laws in chemical reaction engineering. With only (t, A) available, plausible models are single-species effective rate laws (mass-action orders, reversible relaxation to equilibrium, autocatalysis, or time-varying rate coefficients).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate consumption, e.g., surface-limited or saturated catalyst)
- First-order decay (unimolecular): dA_dt = -c0 * A (radioactive/thermal unimolecular-like kinetics, dilute limit)
- Second-order decay (self-reaction): dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular A+A or effective second-order loss)
- General n-th order (power-law): dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical/global rate law over a concentration range)
- Reversible relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to equilibrium concentration A_eq = c1)
- Autocatalytic logistic-type (single-species proxy): dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating formation with finite capacity/limiting reagent proxy)
- Rational (inhibition/saturation in A): dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (self-inhibition or saturation of reactive sites by A)
- Higher-order inhibited: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 / (A**c1 + c2) (rate limited by site coverage or deactivation driven by A)
- Time-dependent rate coefficient (exponential drift): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (catalyst activation/deactivation or temperature program encoded via time)
- Time-dependent rate coefficient (power-law in time): dA_dt = -c0 * t**c1 * A (aging/fouling or diffusion-controlled effective rate changing with time)
- Forcing/production plus decay: dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant feed/formation balanced by first-order loss; well-mixed with source term)
- Periodic modulation (e.g., pulsed illumination): dA_dt = -c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A (externally driven kinetics with periodic rate modulation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If A is monotonically decreasing to ~0 and never changes sign, prefer negative-valued rate laws like -c*A**n with n > 0.
- If initial slope dA_dt at A≈0 is nonzero (finite), include a zero-order term (-c0) or source term (+c0) rather than pure -c*A.
- If A approaches a nonzero plateau, model as relaxation to an equilibrium: dA_dt proportional to (A - A_eq).
- If the magnitude of dA_dt increases at intermediate A but decreases near endpoints, consider autocatalytic forms A*(Amax-A) or inhibited rational forms A/(A+c).
- If the effective rate slows down over time at fixed A (e.g., catalyst deactivation), encode k(t) decreasing with t (e.g., exp(-c*t) or t**(-c) equivalents written as 1/(t**c + c)).
- If the rate accelerates over time at fixed A (activation/heating program), encode k(t) increasing with t (e.g., exp(c*t) or t**c).
- If the data show periodic changes in dA_dt at similar A values, include explicit time forcing via sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) multiplying the A-dependent rate.
- If dA_dt versus A is strongly nonlinear on log-log scale (curvature), prefer mixed structures like A**n/(A**n + c) over a single power law.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK35)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_q*A*log(c2*t + c3)
Candidate formulas: 51

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(t,A)=A\Big(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma\Big)
\]
with \(\alpha=0.062258070344434831\), \(\beta=0.9423435234237035\), \(\gamma=0.13625696690019862\).
So GT is **linear in \(A\)**, has **no additive constant independent of \(A\)**, and its only \(t\)-dependence is through \(\log(\beta t+1)\).

Below, a candidate matches iff we can choose its constants so it becomes exactly \(A(k_1\log(k_2 t+1)+k_0)\) with no extra terms.

1) \(A c0 + A c1 (c2+t)^{c3} + c4\): power term can’t become \(\log\) for all \(t\). Also \(c4\) must be 0. No match.

2) \(A c0 + A c1 \log(c2 t+1)\): choose \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Exact match.

3) \(A c0 + c1\log(c2 t+1)\,|A|\): \(|A|\) cannot equal \(A\) for all real \(A\). No match.

4) \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\): must set \(c3=0\), then same as (2). Match.

5) \(A c0 + A^{c1} c2 \log(c3 t+1)+c4\): need \(c4=0\) and \(A^{c1}\) to be \(A\) for all \(A\), so \(c1=1\). Then set \(c2=\alpha\), \(c3=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Match.

6) \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+A c3 + c4\): set \(c4=0\); combine linear-in-\(A\) constants: \(A(c0+c3)+A c1\log(\cdot)\). Choose \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\), \(c0+c3=-\gamma\). Match.

7) \(A c0 + A c1(c2+t)^{c3} + c4 e^{c5 t}\log(c6|A|+1)\): last term must be 0 ⇒ \(c4=0\). Remaining has power, not log. No match.

8) \(A c0 + A c1\log(\cdot)+c3+c4 t\): need \(c3=c4=0\), then same as (2). Match.

9) \(A c0 + A c1\log(\cdot)+ c3\log(c4 t+1)+c5\): need \(c5=0\) and the extra log term vanish ⇒ \(c3=0\). Then same as (2). Match.

10) Adds rational-in-\(t\) terms plus constant: must set \(c3=c6=c7=0\) to remove them, leaving (2). Match.

11) Has \(A e^{c2 t}\), \(A\sqrt t\), and \(A^{c4}\log\): to reduce to GT must kill exp and sqrt ⇒ \(c1=0,c3=0\). Then need \(A^{c4}\) to be \(A\) ⇒ \(c4=1\), and set \(c5=\alpha,c6=\beta,c0=-\gamma\). Match.

12) Extra \(A c3(c4+t)^{c5}\) and constant \(c6\): set \(c3=0,c6=0\), leaving (2). Match.

13) Similar to 11 but with \(A^{c4} e^{c6 t}\log\): must set \(c1=0,c3=0\); also need \(e^{c6 t}=1\) ⇒ \(c6=0\); need \(A^{c4}=A\) ⇒ \(c4=1\). Then set \(c5=\alpha,c7=\beta,c0=-\gamma\). Match.

14) Extra constant \(c3\) and term \(c4 t (A+c5)^{c6}\): set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then (2). Match.

15) Terms involve \(\log(c3|A|+1)\) and \(|A|^{c6}\): to match GT (linear in \(A\) with no \(|A|\) or \(\log(A)\)), must set \(c1=0\) and \(c4=0\). Then reduces to \(A c0\) only, cannot produce \(A\log(\beta t+1)\). No match.

16) Has extra \(A c3/(A c4+c5)\) and \(c7/(A c4+c5)\) and constant \(c6\): to remove non-GT dependence on \(A\), set \(c3=0,c7=0,c6=0\). Then (2). Match.

17) Has \(A c1/(c2 t+c3)\) and \(c8/(c2 t+c3)\) plus \(A^{c4}c5\log\): must set \(c1=0,c8=0,c7=0\). Need \(A^{c4}=A\) ⇒ \(c4=1\). Then choose \(c5=\alpha,c6=\beta,c0=-\gamma\). Match.

18) Extra \(c3\log(A c4+1)+c5\): must set \(c3=0,c5=0\). Then (2). Match.

19) Contains \(A^2 c0\) and multiple linear \(A\) terms: set \(c0=0\) to remove \(A^2\); combine \(A c1 + A c4\) into constant-in-\(t\) coefficient; set \(c5=0\). Then choose \(c2=\alpha,c3=\beta\) and \(c1+c4=-\gamma\). Match.

20) Extra terms \(A c3/(c4 t+c5)\) and \(c7/(c4 t+c5)\) and constant \(c6\): set \(c3=0,c7=0,c6=0\). Then (2). Match.

21) Has \(A^2 c0\log\) plus \(A c2\) plus \(A c3\log\) plus constant: set \(c0=0,c5=0\). Then choose \(c3=\alpha,c4=\beta\), and \(c2=-\gamma\). Match.

22) Extra \(c3 t^{c4}+c5\): set \(c3=0,c5=0\). Then (2). Match.

23) Extra constant and sine: set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then (2). Match.

24) Extra \(c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\): set \(c3=0,c5=0\). Then (2). Match.

25) Extra \(A c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\): set \(c3=0,c5=0\). Then (2). Match.

26) Extra constant and rational-in-\(A\): set \(c3=0\) and \(c4=0,c7=0\). Then (2). Match.

27) Has \(A e^{c2 t}\), \(A\sqrt t\), and \(A c4(c5+t)^{c6}\): can’t create \(\log\) unless those are removed, but then no log term remains. No match.

28) Extra constant \(c7\) and a Max-based rational term: set \(c3=0,c7=0\). Then (2). Match.

29) Has exp, sqrt, and \(A\log(\log(|t|))\): cannot reduce to \(A\log(\beta t+1)\) by constants alone (even if exp/sqrt killed, remaining log structure wrong). No match.

30) Extra constant and complicated log with \(e^{A c8}\): must set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then (2). Match.

31) Extra constant and \(c4\exp(c5\sin(\cdots))\): set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then (2). Match.

32) Extra constant and \(c4 e^{c5 t}\log(A c6+1)\): set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then (2). Match.

33) Has exp terms and \(A^{c6}c7\log\): set exp-related coefficients to 0: \(c1=0,c3=0\). Need \(A^{c6}=A\) ⇒ \(c6=1\). Then set \(c7=\alpha,c8=\beta,c0=-\gamma\). Match.

34) Extra rational term in \(A\) with \(e^{c5 t}\): set \(c3=0,c7=0\). Then (2). Match.

35) Has \(A t^{c2}\) and \(A^{c3}e^{c5 t}\) and \(A^{c6}e^{c8 t}\log\): to get GT must kill first two terms ⇒ \(c1=0,c4=0\). For last term need \(e^{c8 t}=1\) ⇒ \(c8=0\), and \(A^{c6}=A\) ⇒ \(c6=1\). Then set \(c7=\alpha,c9=\beta,c0=-\gamma\). Match.

36) Extra \(c3\sin(A c4+c5)+c6\): set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Then (2). Match.

37) Extra \(A^{c3}c4+c5\): set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then (2). Match.
